// Parva 1, Adhyaya 0, Verse 0
nārāyaṇaṃ suraguruṃ jagadekanāthaṃ bhaktapriyaṃ sakalalokanamaskṛtaṃ ca traiguṇyavarjitam ajaṃ vibhum ādyam īśaṃ vande bhavaghnam asurāsurasiddhavandyam

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 3
uvāca tān ṛṣīn sarvān dhanyo vo 'smy adya darśanāt veda vaiyāsikīḥ sarvāḥ kathā dharmārthasaṃhitāḥ vakṣyāmi vo dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ śṛṇvantv adya tapodhanāḥ tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 7
evaṃ pṛṣṭo 'bravīt samyag yathāval lomaharṣaṇiḥ vākyaṃ vacanasaṃpannas teṣāṃ tu caritāśrayam tasmin sadasi vistīrṇe munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 14
śrutaṃ me bhāratākhyānaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣadam janamejayena pṛṣṭaḥ san vaiśaṃpāyana uktavān ṛṣīṇām agratas tatra dharmiṣṭhānāṃ mahātmanām vyāsadevājñayā tatra yad vaiśaṃpāyanas tadā śrutaṃ vai bhāratākhyānaṃ vedārthaiś copabṛṃhitam tatra me viditaṃ sarvaṃ bhāratākhyānam āditaḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 23
namo bhagavate tasmai vyāsāyāmitatejase yasya prasādād vakṣyāmi nārāyaṇakathām imām sarvāśramābhigamanaṃ sarvatīrthāvagāhanam na tathā phaladaṃ sūte nārāyaṇakathā yathā nāsti nārāyaṇasamaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati etena satyavākyena sarvārthān sādhayāmy aham

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 26
puṇye himavataḥ pāde medhye giriguhālaye viśodhya dehaṃ dharmātmā darbhasaṃstaram āśritaḥ śuciḥ saniyamo vyāsaḥ śāntātmā tapasi sthitaḥ bhāratasyetihāsasya dharmeṇānvīkṣya tāṃ gatim praviśya yogaṃ jñānena so 'paśyat sarvam antataḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 35

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 47

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 48

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 56

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 60

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 63

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 64

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 69

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 87

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 104

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 106

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 107

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 108

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 110

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 112

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 113

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 118

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 120

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 125

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 145

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 1, Verse 156

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 2, Verse 126
mārkaṇḍeyasya ca tathā devarṣer nāradasya ca tathā yajñavibhūtiś ca gayasyātra prakīrtitā prabhāsatīrthe pāṇḍūnāṃ vṛṣṇibhiś ca samāgamaḥ māndhātuś cāpy upākhyānaṃ rājño 'traiva prakīrtitam aṣṭāvakrasya viprarṣer janakasyādhvare 'bhavat naiyāyikānāṃ mukhyena varuṇasyātmajena hi parājito yatra bandī vāde tena mahātmanā yavakrītasya cākhyānaṃ raibhyasya ca mahātmanaḥ gandhamādanayātrā ca vāso nārāyaṇāśrame vrajan pathi mahābāhur dṛṣṭavān pavanātmajam kadalīkhaṇḍamadhyasthaṃ hanūmantaṃ mahābalam vṛṣaparvaṇaś ca rājarṣes tato 'bhigamanaṃ smṛtam ārṣṭiṣeṇāśrame caiṣāṃ gamanaṃ vāsa eva ca protsāhanaṃ ca pāñcālyā bhīmasyātra mahātmanaḥ kailāsārohaṇaṃ proktaṃ yatra yakṣair balotkaṭaiḥ yuddham āsīn mahāghoraṃ maṇimatpramukhaiḥ saha samāgamaś ca pāṇḍūnāṃ yatra vaiśravaṇena ca samāgamaś cārjunasya tatraiva bhrātṛbhiḥ saha nivātakavacair ghorair dānavaiḥ suraśatrubhiḥ paulomaiḥ kālakeyaiś ca yatra yuddhaṃ kirīṭinaḥ vadhaś caiṣāṃ samākhyāto rājñas tenaiva dhīmatā astrasaṃdarśanārambho dharmarājasya saṃnidhau pārthasya pratiṣedhaś ca nāradena maharṣiṇā avarohaṇaṃ punaś caiva pāṇḍūnāṃ gandhamādanāt bhīmasya grahaṇaṃ cātra parvatābhogavarṣmaṇā bhujagendreṇa balinā tasmin sugahane vane amokṣayad yatra cainaṃ praśnān uktvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kāmyakāgamanaṃ caiva punas teṣāṃ mahātmanām tatrasthāṃś ca punar draṣṭuṃ pāṇḍavān puruṣarṣabhān vāsudevasyāgamanam atraiva parikīrtitam pṛthor vainyasya cākhyānaṃ yatroktaṃ paramarṣiṇā saṃvādaś ca sarasvatyās tārkṣyarṣeḥ sumahātmanaḥ matsyopākhyānam atraiva procyate tadanantaram mārkaṇḍeyasamasyā ca purāṇaṃ parikīrtyate aindradyumnam upākhyānaṃ dhaundhumāraṃ tathaiva ca pativratāyāś cākhyānaṃ tathaivāṅgirasaṃ smṛtam hriyamāṇas tu mandātmā mokṣito 'sau kirīṭinā dharmarājasya cātraiva mṛgasvapnanidarśanam kāmyake kānanaśreṣṭhe punargamanam ucyate vrīhidrauṇikam ākhyānam atraiva bahuvistaram durvāsaso 'py upākhyānam atraiva parikīrtitam cakre cainaṃ pañcaśikhaṃ yatra bhīmo mahābalaḥ yatra rāmeṇa vikramya nihato rāvaṇo yudhi

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 42, Verse 1

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 43, Verse 2

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 46, Verse 18
ahaṃ sa takṣako brahman paśya me vīryam adbhutam na śaktas tvaṃ mayā daṣṭaṃ taṃ saṃjīvayituṃ nṛpam ity uktvā takṣakas tatra so 'daśad vai vanaspatim sa daṣṭamātro nāgena bhasmībhūto 'bhavan nagaḥ kāśyapaś ca tato rājann ajīvayata taṃ nagam tatas taṃ lobhayām āsa kāmaṃ brūhīti takṣakaḥ sa evam uktas taṃ prāha kāśyapas takṣakaṃ punaḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 46, Verse 25
etasminn eva kāle tu sa rājā janamejayaḥ uvāca mantriṇaḥ sarvān idaṃ vākyam ariṃdamaḥ atha tat kathitaṃ kena yad vṛttaṃ tad vanaspatau āścaryabhūtaṃ lokasya bhasmarāśīkṛtaṃ tadā yad vṛkṣaṃ jīvayām āsa kāśyapas takṣakeṇa vai nūnaṃ mantrair hataviṣo na praṇaśyeta kāśyapāt cintayām āsa pāpātmā manasā pannagādhamaḥ daṣṭaṃ yadi mayā vipraḥ pārthivaṃ jīvayiṣyati takṣakaḥ saṃhataviṣo loke yāsyati hāsyatām vicintyaivaṃ kṛtā tena dhruvaṃ tuṣṭir dvijasya vai bhaviṣyati hy upāyena yasya dāsyāmi yātanām

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 46, Verse 37

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 51, Verse 9

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 51, Verse 11

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 51, Verse 23

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 55, Verse 18

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 55, Verse 21
sutapriyaiṣī tān rājā pāṇḍavān ambikāsutaḥ (17ab) tato vivāsayām āsa rājyabhogabubhukṣayā te prātiṣṭhanta sahitā nagarān nāgasāhvayāt prasthāne cābhavan mantrī kṣattā teṣāṃ mahātmanām yena muktā jatugṛhān niśīthe prādravan vanam tataḥ saṃprāpya kaunteyā nagaraṃ vāraṇāvatam nyavasanta mahātmāno mātrā saha paraṃtapāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa cājñaptā uṣitā jātuṣe gṛhe purocanād rakṣamāṇāḥ saṃvatsaram atandritāḥ (18ab) suruṅgāṃ kārayitvā te vidureṇa pracoditāḥ ādīpya jātuṣaṃ veśma dagdhvā caiva purocanam (18cd) prādravan bhayasaṃvignā mātrā saha paraṃtapāḥ (19ab) dadṛśur dāruṇaṃ rakṣo hiḍimbaṃ vananirjhare hatvā ca taṃ rākṣasendraṃ bhītāḥ samanubodhanāt niśi saṃprādravan pārthā dhārtarāṣṭrabhayārditāḥ (20ab) ekacakrāṃ tato gatvā pāṇḍavāḥ saṃśitavratāḥ (20cd) vedādhyayanasaṃpannās te 'bhavan brahmacāriṇaḥ te tatra prayatāḥ kālaṃ kaṃ cid ūṣur nararṣabhāḥ mātrā sahaikacakrāyāṃ brāhmaṇasya niveśane tatrāsasāda kṣudhitaṃ puruṣādaṃ vṛkodaraḥ (21ab) bhīmaseno mahābāhur bakaṃ nāma mahābalam taṃ cāpi puruṣavyāghro bāhuvīryeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ nihatya tarasā vīro nāgarān paryasāntvayat tatas te śuśruvuḥ kṛṣṇāṃ pañcāleṣu svayaṃvarām śrutvā caivābhyagacchanta gatvā caivālabhanta tām

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 55, Verse 31

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 56, Verse 13

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 69, Verse 26

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 69, Verse 43
sa mātaram upasthāya rathantaryām abhāṣata mama putro vane jātas tava śokapraṇāśanaḥ ṛṇād adya vimukto 'haṃ tava pautreṇa śobhane viśvāmitrasutā ceyaṃ kaṇvena ca vivardhitā snuṣā tava mahābhāge prasīdasva śakuntalām putrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā pautraṃ sā pariṣasvaje pādayoḥ patitāṃ tatra rathantaryā śakuntalām pariṣvajya ca bāhubhyāṃ harṣād aśrūṇy avartayat uvāca vacanaṃ satyaṃ lakṣaye lakṣaṇāni ca tava putro viśālākṣi cakravartī bhaviṣyati tava bhartā viśālākṣi trailokyavijayī bhavet divyān bhogān anuprāptā bhava tvaṃ varavarṇini evam uktā rathantaryā paraṃ harṣam avāpa sā śakuntalāṃ tato rājā śāstroktenaiva karmaṇā tato 'gramahiṣīṃ kṛtvā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitām brāhmaṇebhyo dhanaṃ dattvā sainikānāṃ ca bhūpatiḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 70, Verse 44

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 73, Verse 23

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 74, Verse 6

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 76, Verse 27

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 76, Verse 35

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 77, Verse 4

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 77, Verse 6

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 89, Verse 55

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 90, Verse 96

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 92, Verse 18

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 96, Verse 6

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 98, Verse 13

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 98, Verse 16

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 98, Verse 17
dharmātmā ca mahātmā ca vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ godharmaṃ saurabheyāc ca so 'dhītya nikhilaṃ muniḥ prāvartata tathā kartuṃ śraddhāvāṃs tam aśaṅkayā tato vitathamaryādaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā munisattamāḥ kruddhā mohābhibhūtās te sarve tatrāśramaukasaḥ aho 'yaṃ bhinnamaryādo nāśrame vastum arhati tasmād enaṃ vayaṃ sarve pāpātmānaṃ tyajāmahe ity anyonyaṃ samābhāṣya te dīrghatamasaṃ munim

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 98, Verse 19

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 98, Verse 22

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 98, Verse 32

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 99, Verse 4

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 99, Verse 5

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 99, Verse 9

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 99, Verse 11

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 99, Verse 12

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 103, Verse 17

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 198, Verse 13

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 198, Verse 19

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 199, Verse 14

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 199, Verse 24

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 199, Verse 26

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 199, Verse 27

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 199, Verse 28

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 199, Verse 34

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 199, Verse 36

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 199, Verse 39

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 199, Verse 46

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 213, Verse 22

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 214, Verse 29
siṃhāsanasamīpe tau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 214, Verse 31
jagāma tau kṛṣṇapārthau didhakṣan khāṇḍavaṃ vanam

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 214, Verse 32
dṛṣṭvā jagāma manasā pāvako 'yam iti prabhuḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 215, Verse 8
bahūni ghorarūpāṇi ugravīryāṇi caiva hi

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 215, Verse 12
abravīn nṛpaśārdūla tatkālasadṛśaṃ vacaḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 215, Verse 15
upāsaṃgau ca me na staḥ pratiyoddhuṃ puraṃdaram

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 216, Verse 3
tvam asmai savyasācine divyair aśvaiḥ samāyuktaṃ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 216, Verse 7
tad divyaṃ dhanuṣāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ brahmaṇā nirmitaṃ purā

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 216, Verse 11
surāriyoṣitsauvarṇaśrutitāṭaṅkanāśanam

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 216, Verse 13
yaḥ purā vāyusaṃbhūto rakṣogaṇavināśanaḥ nādena ca mahāraudro bhūtakoṭisamāvṛtaḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 216, Verse 16
viṣṇor ājñāṃ gṛhītvā tu phalgunaḥ paravīrahā

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 216, Verse 29
sa surāsuramānavān kiṃ punar vajriṇaikaṃ tu

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 216, Verse 30
yadi khāṇḍavam eṣyati pramādāt sagaṇo vā parirakṣituṃ mahendraḥ śaratāḍitakhaṇḍakuṇḍalānāṃ kadanaṃ drakṣyati devavāhinīnām

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 217, Verse 13
upalabhya samutpetuḥ samutpetur mahīdharāt

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 217, Verse 14
tenārciṣā susaṃtaptā devāḥ sarṣipurogamāḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 217, Verse 16
ity ākrośam akurvaṃs te lokāḥ sarve bhayānvitāḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 218, Verse 3
tad dṛṣṭvā vāritaṃ toyaṃ nārācaiḥ savyasācinā āścaryam agaman devā munayaś ca divi sthitāḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 218, Verse 13
subhadrajavam ādīptaṃ tadā vāyuṃ visarja ha

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 218, Verse 14
tato 'śanimuco ghorāṃs taḍitstanitaniḥsvanān

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 218, Verse 18
sicyamāno vasaughais taiḥ prāṇināṃ dehaniḥsṛtaiḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 218, Verse 21
tāṃś cārkasadṛśair astraiḥ parapakṣasamāśritān

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 218, Verse 27
śerate rudhiraklinnā indragopakasaṃnibhāḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 218, Verse 31
śaktiṃ khaḍgaṃ yāturājaḥ samīro 'ṅkuśam eva ca

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 219, Verse 3
te vanaṃ prasamīkṣyātha dahyamānam anekadhā kṛṣṇam abhyudyatāstraṃ ca nādaṃ mumucur ulbaṇam tena nādena raudreṇa nādena ca vibhāvasoḥ rarāsa gaganaṃ kṛtsnam utpātajaladair iva tataḥ kṛṣṇo mahābāhuḥ svatejo bhāsvaraṃ mahat

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 219, Verse 36
jñātvā taṃ dānavendrāṇāṃ mayaṃ vai śilpināṃ varam

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 219, Verse 38
taṃ na bhetavyam ity āha mayaṃ pārtho dayāparaḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 219, Verse 39
tad vanaṃ pāvako dhīmān dināni daśa pañca ca dadāha kṛṣṇapārthābhyāṃ rakṣitaḥ pākaśāsanāt

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 220, Verse 4
tasmin vane dahyamāne sarvabhūtabhayaṃkaraḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 220, Verse 10
āpnomi saphalāṃl lokāṃs tat karma brūta māciram

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 220, Verse 21
maharṣir mandapālo 'sau vadhāt stotuṃ pracakrame

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 220, Verse 29
mama putrāṃś ca pautrāṃś ca patnīṃ rakṣa hutāśana gṛhaṃ kṣetraṃ paśūn rakṣa rakṣa māṃ sarva sarvadā jarāyuṇāvṛtaṃ garbhaṃ pāsi deva jagatpate tvam ātmā jagataḥ stutyo devadeva namo 'stu te

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 220, Verse 31
bhāryāṃ rakṣa gṛhaṃ rakṣa paśuṃ me rakṣa sarvadā patantu hetayaḥ sarve svanyad asmat tavābhibho sarvatra sarvadāsmākaṃ śivo bhava hutāśana

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 221, Verse 6
kathaṃ pradīptāj jvalanād vimucyeran sutā mama mandabhāgyā saputrāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi śocatī

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 221, Verse 9
sahaiva carituṃ bālair na śaknomi tapovane

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 221, Verse 21
agnidāhe tu niyataṃ brahmaloke dhruvā gatiḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 222, Verse 6
namo 'stu te śyenarāja rakṣitā rājavat tvayā

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 222, Verse 15
samāgamaś ca bhavitā tvaṃ vai śokaṃ ca mā kṛthāḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 222, Verse 18
vyathitāḥ karuṇā vācaḥ śrāvayām āsur antikāt

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 223, Verse 1
kathaṃ nāma pitāsmākaṃ duḥkhāpannā vaśaṃtvite (sic)

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 223, Verse 24
tvadbhaktān sarvadeveśa jātavedo mahāyaśāḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 224, Verse 19
jaritā tu pariṣvajya putrasnehād acumbata

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 224, Verse 20
gurutvān mandapālasya iti pādāntikaṃ gatāḥ abhivādayāmahe sarve jātapakṣāḥ prasādataḥ evam uktavatāṃ teṣāṃ pratinandya mahātapāḥ pariṣvajya ca tān putrān mūrdhny upāghrāya bālakān putrasparśāt tu yā prītis tām avāpa sa gautamaḥ

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 224, Verse 23
evam uktvā tu tāṃ patnīṃ mandapālas tathāspṛśat

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 224, Verse 26
strīṇāṃ sadā hi sāpatnyaṃ bhavitavyaṃ hi tat tathā

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 225, Verse 9
astraṃ pāśupataṃ deva vṛṇomi vadatāṃ vara divyāny astrāṇi cānyāni dadasva harivāhana aindrādīn gṛhyatāṃ pārtha astrāṇi vidhipūrvakam astraṃ pāśupataṃ divyaṃ tryambakas te pradāsyati

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 225, Verse 17
gāṇḍīvaṃ ca dhanur divyam akṣayyau ca maheṣudhī kapidhvajo rathaś cāyaṃ tava dattau mahāratha anena dhanuṣā caiva rathenānena bhārata vijeṣyasi raṇe śatrūn sasurāsuramānuṣān

// Parva 1, Adhyaya 225, Verse 19
tato 'bravīn mayaḥ pārthaṃ vāsudevasya saṃnidhau prāñjaliḥ ślakṣṇayā vācā pūjayitvā punaḥ punaḥ
